        <script src="https://clark.com/wp-content/themes/clark/inc/plugins/menu-features/accessibleMegaMenu.js?"></script>

        <script>

            
            (function( $ ) {

                var $body = $('body'),
                    $subNavContainer = $('[data-sub-nav]'),
                    $mainNavContainer = $('[data-main-nav]'),
                    $mainNavContainerList = $('[data-main-nav] > ul');
                    $mainNavItem = $('[data-main-nav-item]');
                    $subNavHeader = $('[data-sub-nav-header]');
                    $mainMenuToggle = $('[data-menu-toggle]');

                    _menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[data-main-nav-item]');

                var ARROW_DOWN = 40,
                    ARROW_UP = 38,
                    ARROW_LEFT = 37,
                    ARROW_RIGHT = 39,
                    TAB = 9;
                var subMenusShown = false;

                if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 992px)').matches) {

                    wideScreenFncs();

                } else {

                    narrowScreenFncs();
                }

                window.matchMedia('(min-width: 992px)').onchange = function (event) {

                    if(event.matches){

                        // WIDE SCREEN
                        wideScreenFncs();

                    }
                    else if( !event.matches) {

                        // NARROW SCREEN
                        narrowScreenFncs();

                    }
                };

                function narrowScreenFncs() {

                    // reset subnavs
                    $subNavContainer.removeClass('is-active-wide');
                    $subNavContainer.removeClass('open');
                    $('[data-sub-nav]')
                        .css({
                            visibility: "visible",
                            top: 0,
                            opacity: 1,
                            left: 'auto'
                        });

                    // turn off wide handlers
                    $mainNavContainer.off("mouseenter mouseleave");
                    $mainNavItem.off("mouseenter mouseleave");

                    // Toggle mobile toggle & main mav
                    $mainMenuToggle.on('click', function(e){

                       e.preventDefault();

                        if($mainNavContainer.hasClass('is-active')){
                            onCloseMenu();
                        } else{
                            $(this).addClass('is-active');
                            $mainNavContainer.addClass("is-active");

                            $(this).addClass('open');
                            $mainNavContainer.addClass('open');

                            $body.addClass('mobile-menu-active');
                            $mainNavContainerList.addClass('is-showing-main');
                        }

                        // var docElemStyle = document.documentElement.style;
                        // var transitionProp = typeof docElemStyle.transition == 'string' ? 'transition' : 'WebkitTransition';
                        //
                        // for ( var i=0; i < _menuItems.length; i++ ) {
                        //     var item = _menuItems[i];
                        //     // stagger transition with transitionDelay
                        //     item.style[ transitionProp + 'Delay' ] = ( i * 50 ) + 'ms';
                        //     item.classList.toggle('is-moved');
                        // }

                    });

                    // Toggle subnav
                    $mainNavItem.on('click', function(e) {

                        e.preventDefault();

                        var $this = $(this),
                            navItemDataId = $this.data("main-nav-item"),
                            $navItemParent = $this.parent('.nav-item'),
                            $subNavDiv = $('div').find("[data-div='" + navItemDataId + "']");

                            // $('.nav-item').not($navItemParent).addClass('is-hidden-item');

                            $('.nav-item').css({visibility: 'visible'});

                        if($subNavDiv.hasClass('is-active-narrow')) {
                            $mainNavContainerList.addClass('is-showing-main');
                            $subNavDiv.removeClass('is-active-narrow');

                        } else {
                            $mainNavContainerList.removeClass('is-showing-main');
                            $subNavDiv.addClass('is-active-narrow');
                            $('.nav-item').not($navItemParent).css({
                                visibility: 'hidden'
                            })
                        }
                    });

                    // click outside, close menu
                    $(document).on('click', function closeMainMenu(e) {

                        if ( ! $mainNavContainer.is(e.target) && $mainNavContainer.has(e.target).length === 0 && ! $mainMenuToggle.is(e.target) && $mainMenuToggle.has(e.target).length === 0 ) {

                            onCloseMenu();

                        }
                    });

                    // Close menu and remove all classes
                    function onCloseMenu() {
                        $mainNavContainer.removeClass('is-active');
                        $mainMenuToggle.removeClass('is-active');
                        $body.removeClass('mobile-menu-active');

                        $mainNavContainer.removeClass('open');
                        $mainMenuToggle.removeClass('open');
                    }

                }


                ///
                //
                //
                //
                // WIDE
                //
                //
                //
                //

                function wideScreenFncs() {

                    // Turn off mobile handlers
                    $mainMenuToggle.off('click');
                    $mainNavItem.off('click');
                    $mainNavContainer.removeClass("is-active");
                    $mainMenuToggle.removeClass("is-active");

                    $mainNavContainer.removeClass("open");
                    $mainMenuToggle.removeClass("open");

                    // reset sub navs
                    $subNavContainer.removeClass('is-active-narrow');
                    $subNavContainer.removeClass('open');
                    $('[data-sub-nav]')
                        .css({
                            visibility: "hidden",
                            top: 0,
                            opacity: 0,
                            left: 'auto'
                        });


                    $('[data-main-nav]').on({

                        mouseleave: function () {

                            // Reset position and vis of subnavs
                            $subNavContainer.css({visibility: 'hidden', left: 0});

                            $('[data-main-nav-item]').removeClass('is-active-wide');
                            $('[data-main-nav-item]').removeClass('open');

                        }
                    });

                    function showMainNav($this) {

                        var navItemDataId = $this.data("main-nav-item"),
                                leftSideMainNavItem = $this.position().left,
                                $subNavDiv = $('div').find("[data-div='" + navItemDataId + "']");

                            // Inactivate all other main menu items
                            $('[data-main-nav-item]').not($this).removeClass('is-active-wide');
                            $('[data-main-nav-item]').not($this).removeClass('open');

                            // // Hide any open sub navs
                            $('[data-sub-nav]').not($subNavDiv).css({visibility: 'hidden', left: 0});

                            if (!$this.hasClass('is-active-wide')) {

                                subMenusShown = true;

                                $this.addClass('is-active-wide');

                                $subNavDiv.addClass('is-active-wide');

                                $this.addClass('open');

                                $subNavDiv.addClass('open');

                                // show the subnav for this menu item
                                $subNavDiv
                                    .css({
                                        visibility: "visible",
                                        top: "calc(100% + 20px)",
                                        opacity: 0,
                                        left: leftSideMainNavItem
                                    })
                                    .stop()
                                    .animate({
                                        top: '100%',
                                        opacity: 1
                                    }, 200);

                            }
                    }

                    function processKeys($this, event) {
                        if (event.keyCode === ARROW_DOWN || event.keyCode === ARROW_UP || event.keyCode === ARROW_LEFT || event.keyCode === ARROW_RIGHT || event.keyCode === TAB) {

                            // To do how Adobe does it (which is referenced in the plugin), only nav completely through submenus once the user sees at least one
                            if (event.keyCode === TAB && !subMenusShown) {
                                return;
                            }
                            showMainNav($this);
                        }
                    }
                    $('[data-main-nav-item]').on("keydown", function (event) {
                        processKeys($(this), event);
                    });
                    $('[data-main-nav-item]').on("keyup", function (event) {
                        processKeys($(this), event);
                    });

                    $('[data-main-nav-item]').on("mouseenter mouseleave", function (event) {

                        var $this = $(this),
                            docWidth = document.documentElement.offsetWidth,
                            navItemDataId = $this.data("main-nav-item"),
                            $subNavDiv = $('div').find("[data-div='" + navItemDataId + "']"),
                            leftSideMainNavItem = $this.position().left;

                        if (event.type === "mouseenter") {

                            // if Subnav is offscreen, adjust its position to align right side of menu item
                            var rightSideSubNavDiv = $subNavDiv[0].getBoundingClientRect().right;

                            if (rightSideSubNavDiv > docWidth) {
                                leftSideMainNavItem = -($subNavDiv.outerWidth() - $this.outerWidth());
                            }

                            showMainNav($this);
                            // // Inactivate all other main menu items
                            // $('[data-main-nav-item]').not($this).removeClass('is-active-wide');
                            // $('[data-main-nav-item]').not($this).removeClass('open');

                            // // Hide any open sub navs
                            // $('[data-sub-nav]').not($subNavDiv).css({visibility: 'hidden', left: 0});

                            // if (!$this.hasClass('is-active-wide')) {

                            //     $this.addClass('is-active-wide');

                            //     $subNavDiv.addClass('is-active-wide');

                            //     $this.addClass('open');

                            //     $subNavDiv.addClass('open');

                            //     // show the subnav for this menu item
                            //     $subNavDiv
                            //         .css({
                            //             visibility: "visible",
                            //             top: "calc(100% + 20px)",
                            //             opacity: 0,
                            //             left: leftSideMainNavItem
                            //         })
                            //         .stop()
                            //         .animate({
                            //             top: '100%',
                            //             opacity: 1
                            //         }, 200);

                            // }

                        }
                        else if (event.type === "mouseleave") {


                            if (!$subNavDiv.hasClass('is-active-wide')) {
                                $this.removeClass('is-active-wide');

                                $this.removeClass('open');
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }

                // ------------ Accessible ----------------
                $("nav:first").accessibleMegaMenu({
                            /* prefix for generated unique id attributes, which are required 
                            to indicate aria-owns, aria-controls and aria-labelledby */
                            uuidPrefix: "accessible-megamenu",
                            
                            /* css class used to define the megamenu styling */
                            menuClass: "nav-menu",
                            
                            /* css class for a top-level navigation item in the megamenu */
                            topNavItemClass: "nav-item",
                            
                            /* css class for a megamenu panel */
                            panelClass: "sub-nav",
                            
                            /* css class for a group of items within a megamenu panel */
                            panelGroupClass: "sub-nav-group",
                            
                            /* css class for the hover state */
                            hoverClass: "hover",
                            
                            /* css class for the focus state */
                            focusClass: "focus",
                            
                            /* css class for the open state */
                            openClass: "open"
                        });
                // ----------------------------------------
                
            })(jQuery);

        </script>

	</div>

    });

    window.onclick = function (event) {
        if (!event.target.matches('.cp-other')) {
            if (dropdownContent.style.display === 'block') {
                dropdownContent.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    }


</script>

        var ua= navigator.userAgent, tem,
        M= ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie|trident(?=\/))\/?\s*(\d+)/i) || [];
        if(/trident/i.test(M[1])){
            tem=  /\brv[ :]+(\d+)/g.exec(ua) || [];

        }
        if(M[1]=== 'Chrome'){
            tem= ua.match(/\b(OPR|Edge)\/(\d+)/);
            if(tem!= null) return tem.slice(1).join(' ').replace('OPR', 'Opera');

        return M.join(' ');
    }
